\DoxyCodeLine{55   \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_1_1internal_1_1maglev_ac85096c0fed967b01a054a97502fe592a016a4c677dea4af4b6898d79b133c29f}{kRemove}},     \textcolor{comment}{// Remove the current node from the graph (and do not call the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{56                \textcolor{comment}{// following processors).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{57   \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_1_1internal_1_1maglev_ac85096c0fed967b01a054a97502fe592acf2da3ccecdd3386e4ebd48f7f4d2690}{kHoist}},      \textcolor{comment}{// Hoist the current instruction to the parent basic block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{58                \textcolor{comment}{// and reset the current instruction to the beginning of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{59                \textcolor{comment}{// block. Parent block must be dominating.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{60   \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_1_1internal_1_1maglev_ac85096c0fed967b01a054a97502fe592a4bd1defe370d56ac49e5719a12e25f7b}{kAbort}},      \textcolor{comment}{// Stop processing now, do not process subsequent nodes/blocks.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{61                \textcolor{comment}{// Should not be used when processing Constants.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{62   \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_1_1internal_1_1maglev_ac85096c0fed967b01a054a97502fe592aa244241f1c36271914fd4e601cd3b895}{kSkipBlock}},  \textcolor{comment}{// Stop processing this block and skip the remaining nodes (no}}
\DoxyCodeLine{63                \textcolor{comment}{// MultiProcessor support).}}
